This is what she longed for, her heart still fiercely red. (Dreamlike, blind, and elaborately extended love is equal to no love; love is possessive, the heart is singular!) Because of the restlessness of her soul and the trivialization of reason, even if she had more than anyone else, the eyes of love harbor venom; they cannot allow a third party to participate. Thus, under a resolute affirmation, she tiptoed out of the human world. The sun, air, and water were the objects of her pursuit, even if she was intertwined with poverty, pain, and a degree of emaciation that was difficult to gauge. Currently, nature is her only companion; she is not lonely, but she feels solitary. Since ancient times, no great philosopher has not become a philosophical figure through great solitude. The pressing force of great solitude often leads people to the pessimistic perspective of "all is emptiness" because the decline of life feels painful. The decline of vitality usually stems from dissatisfaction in life. For women, it is mostly due to heartbreak or dissatisfaction with their families. Further, the stimulation that society gives will cause women to fall into the so-called philosophy of pessimism. The philosophy of stoicism and the retaliatory philosophy of Lao Zhuang, as well as ancient Chinese poets, were her only good friends during her seclusion. No matter how many philosophical theories or ways to find self-deliverance there may be, physiology influences psychology. Finally, she fell into Schopenhauer's view: "The real human world has become an incurable abyss of all evils, and it is further deteriorated by the impulse of will (fame and fortune). The best policy is to clear the mind and destroy the will to seek the ultimate bliss of spiritual ascension." Thus, in a helpless and desolate situation, on a cold early winter night, she listened to the wild rain outside the window, reciting Lu Fangweng's poem "Feeling After Reading a Book on a Spring Night." "My dead bones will decay, and the annals of history will have no name. If this poem is not written, who will understand my loyal heart?" "Wanting to talk about old things with no one to share, as the sun sets, crows return and I lean on the tower again." Even if she strives for her so-called career, in the currently abnormally developed world, women's position in social competition is still small and insignificant. Therefore, a woman with a strong will to search for self-expression after the disillusionment of a fantasy, awakening from the petty love of the human world and pursuing a so-called career, will gradually die of depression in a corner room of a cold village. On a Yangtze River Steamer Zhou Han On a Yangtze River boat, because the wind was calm and the waves were smooth, there was no seasickness at all. My eyes were often open, looking everywhere, and my ears were often listening, so my knowledge and experience were greatly broadened. When the boat arrived in Wuhu, just as it docked at the pier, a middle-aged woman came into our room to stay. Originally, it was just me and a female student from Nanjing who were going home together, so there were three people, filling all three berths in the room. The female student from Nanjing, a girl in her teens, was innocent and clever. I got along well with her. Now that this middle-aged woman came in, seeing her face covered with dust, she seemed to be someone who frequented the rivers and lakes, with an experienced look. It made people feel uncomfortable at first sight. The little girl signaled to me with her eyes, making a face. She was not happy about this middle-aged woman. I wasn't happy either. Moreover, the upper and lower berths in front of the window had already been occupied by the two of us. The berth next to it was originally for us to put our boxes and baskets, but as soon as she came in, the waiter put our boxes and baskets on the ground and under the berth. How annoying! The woman brought a suitcase and a bedding roll with her. As soon as she entered the room, she told the waiter to open the bedding and spread it out, then lay down on it. She casually took out a pack of Hardman cigarettes from her small straw bag, lit one, and started smoking. You know, I get dizzy as soon as I smell cigarette smoke, so what could I do? The little girl was a student and also afraid of cigarette smoke. We were both very unhappy. The little girl was young and didn't dare to interfere, so she just opened the window to ventilate the air and covered her nose and mouth with a handkerchief. But I couldn't stand it, coughed a little, and said to the woman, "Excuse me, we are afraid of cigarette smoke, please go outside to smoke." The woman was very worldly-wise and sensible, and immediately replied, "Oh, I didn't know, sorry, sorry." She immediately stood up, opened the door, and went outside. In my life, I am not afraid of people who are unreasonable. This time, when the woman became reasonable, I felt embarrassed. I felt that she was also a passenger on the boat, and I was just a woman on the boat. Now that we had driven her outside, hadn't we deprived her of her freedom? Moreover, hadn't we two become the masters, and she become an irrelevant person? I was inexplicably lost in thought and wild thoughts. The little girl happily said to me, "She's still obedient, isn't she?" I nodded to show agreement, but couldn't say anything. What could I say, right? After the boat sailed, the woman looked for an opportunity to talk to us, asking us where we were going, where we came from, and what school we were studying at. Her attitude was so sincere, gentle, humble, and polite. Every sentence called us "Miss," and she even thought we were sisters, calling me "Eldest Miss" and the little girl "Second Miss." Could we refuse to talk to her? Of course not, so we talked and talked until we became familiar. When the boat was about to reach Anqing, she looked at the dock by the side of the boat, as if waiting for someone. As soon as the boat docked, a big man followed her into the room. She opened the box, took out a package of things, and handed it to the man. This made me suspicious. What was in the package? It must be smuggled goods. A smuggler evading taxes! After the boat sailed, I asked her what was in the package. She smiled and said, "You students are good people. To tell you the truth, I am a business person. That package is business." So it really was smuggled goods. She sighed about the hardships of life and said that she had no choice but to do this illegal thing. She said that her husband used to do this business, but he was imprisoned after being sued. She had a son and a mother at home, and the family had to eat, so she had no choice but to come out and take the risk for her husband. She envied us for being misses, who had cultivated virtue in their previous lives and were enjoying blessings in this life... I sympathized with her situation, and I was worried about her. A woman like this is also worthy of admiration. How capable! This trip on the river has broadened my horizons. Amateur Mailbox (1) The Problem of Dividing Property Among Brothers Mr. Editor: There are three brothers. Before their father died, because the father was old and the mother died early, all the household affairs were managed by the eldest brother, and the two younger brothers studied outside, with the family providing tuition. Now that the father has died, the brothers all plan to divide the inheritance and establish their own households. However, when dividing the family, the two younger brothers said that the eldest brother had secretly saved a large sum of money while managing the household affairs (there is evidence), but the eldest brother denied this. At the same time, the eldest brother is married, and the two younger brothers are not yet married, so the younger brothers also requested that some money be set aside for their marriage expenses, and the remaining amount be divided equally. The eldest brother refused, which led to disputes. The two younger brothers decided to jointly seek a legal solution. The three brothers are all my friends, and I sincerely hope that they can settle the matter peacefully, so I especially write to you, hoping that you can provide a method to avoid going to court. Wang Yanchen Editor's Note: The inheritance issue raised by Mr. Wang is complex in content, and the editor cannot give a hasty answer based on the brief situation described. Moreover, this kind of legal dispute cannot be resolved by empty words. Therefore, it is best if both parties can understand each other and settle the matter peacefully. If the two younger brothers are determined to fight for the inheritance, they can change their approach and consult a lawyer with detailed information and evidence of the eldest brother's embezzlement, and proceed accordingly. However, the editor has an opinion on inheritance: it is believed that unearned inheritance can only cultivate people's habits of enjoying and squandering. It can also extinguish the spirit of youth and progress, and if used improperly, it is actually harmful and useless. Therefore, it is hoped that the brothers will not be concerned about the inheritance dispute, but should pay close attention to their own future and strive to achieve the goal of self-reliance. Otherwise, even with a rich inheritance, it will never last. (2) How to Learn Mandarin Mr. Editor: There are different dialects in various parts of our country, and language often causes misunderstandings. Therefore, I sincerely hope that the people of the whole country can fully implement Mandarin, which would bring many benefits. However, I myself cannot speak a single sentence of Mandarin, and I suffer greatly when talking to others, and I am especially envious of others' fluent Mandarin. Therefore, I am actively trying to learn Mandarin, but I feel that I want to learn but have no way to start. I think that you, sir, are a teacher for the people, and you should be able to solve my difficulties, so I especially write to you, hoping that you can indicate the path to learning Mandarin and introduce one or two Mandarin guidance books with self-study materials. If you agree, I will be extremely grateful. Respectfully, Bai Yu Editor's Note: To learn Mandarin, you can often talk to people who speak Mandarin, and then work hard to study on your own, and you will eventually achieve this goal over time. There is no special path. Regarding Mandarin guidance books with self-study materials, there are very few now. As for books teaching Mandarin phonetic symbols, although there are some, but at a time when these phonetic symbols are not very developed, except for a few elementary school textbooks, most other books do not use these symbols, so even if you have learned them, it doesn't seem to be of much use at present. If you want to learn this, you can buy "How to Use Mandarin Phonetic Symbols" or "Complete Book of Phonetic Symbols" from Zhonghua Book Company and take a look. It is best to have someone to guide you, otherwise it will be difficult to see results. Shen Bao Local Supplement Architecture Weekly Architecture of the Middle Ages (Part 1) Qin We already know the history of the development of European architecture, its origin and development, and it was very prosperous as early as two thousand years ago. Art architecture spread from Egypt to Mesopotamia, then to Greece, and then the Romans promoted and carried forward their architecture. Thus, Europe has the world's famous and great architecture. But before the Greek style of architecture rose in France, there was an indestructible history in between. At this time, the Europeans were all moved by the craze for architecture, and they wanted to rival the cathedrals of Rome. But generally speaking, most of their architectural styles were pseudo-Roman, and they lacked the Roman spirit of decisiveness and courage. The people of other European nations did not know how the Romans made cement at this time, so they could not use concrete to build houses. They envied the Roman method of dome construction, so they also used small stones and bricks to imitate it. This was most prevalent in northern Italy and southern France. They did not know that the towering dome required an extremely solid pier, like the Romans' thick walls or a type of support column like the Greeks, to support the entire weight. So as a result, the buildings they built were all destroyed and could not be passed down. Although, from the general shape, scope, and carvings of these buildings, we always feel that the perseverance of the designers of this era was not bad, and their ambition can be said to be much stronger than their technology. Later, we gradually discovered steel arch ribs. The construction method of steel was used by the Romans to increase the strength of concrete, but other Europeans did not understand the construction method of steel concrete. They only used steel to support the weight of the joints of the arch ribs and the protruding parts of the house. This kind of construction method unknowingly led them to the path of Gothic style. However, the change of this architectural style cannot be explained by a single reason or aspect, because the change of architectural style must also require the designer's persistent spirit, sensitive talent, and far-sighted vision to succeed. Gothic architecture is full of powerful beauty, and this power is fluid, expressing a balanced combination, which is different from the static and harmonious beauty of Roman architecture. At the same time, its design pays much attention to the height of the building. We can imagine that many buildings at that time mostly had a high tower standing in the clouds, looking down on everything on the ground. The method and materials of construction are two very important points in Gothic design. We know that the Romans liked to use a kind of camouflage method to hide the rough parts inside. In the Gothic style, architects no longer use camouflage methods to seek the beauty of the building. They like to pay attention to the organization of materials and the inseparable and unified nature of each part. Sometimes they prefer to use unbalanced or asymmetrical architectural forms, which can often show a unique aesthetic. New Residential Architecture and Sanitary Design Xi Hao The importance of sanitary design in new residential architecture can be said to have been completely ignored by architects a dozen years ago. In recent years, although this issue has gradually been valued by general engineers, it still fails to be as "sanitary" as possible in actual architectural design. This is an important responsibility that current engineers cannot shirk. We know that residential architecture is the daily residence of ordinary people. Its sanitary design is related to the health of each resident. At the same time, it can also affect the health of other adjacent units. Therefore, European and American architects regard this "sanitary design" as a prerequisite for residential architecture, which is also a feature of 20th century architecture, and it is worth our attention and research. The first issue of sanitary design in new residential architecture is of course the issue of "air." Air is something that people cannot lack for a moment, as everyone knows, but how to replace an appropriate amount of fresh air in residential architecture is really a big problem in architecture. In smog-filled cities, obtaining an appropriate amount of clean air for ventilation is a problem that general engineers find difficult to solve. Although automatic ventilation fans can replace the fresh air in the room, they cannot eliminate all the smoke and dust and gases saturated in the air. Now, larger residential buildings in European and American countries are equipped with small air compressors. The outside air is first compressed to wash away all kinds of smoke and other impurities, and then piped into various parts of the house, and the used air is disposed of. Although this system is good, it is not suitable for small-scale residences. For the sake of economic requirements, in addition to installing automatic ventilation fans, an air purifier is installed behind this fan, which is a very fine return copper mesh, which can prevent the passage of extremely fine smoke or unclean particles in the air. However, it is impossible to isolate all odorous gases (such as carbon dioxide and sulfur trioxide in automobile exhaust). Now, although some engineers have invented a method of coating certain compounds on air purifiers to remove these gases, it is still in the experimental stage, and we can hardly predict the results. The only remedy at present is to plant evergreen trees around the house, because they have a very strong natural cleaning effect, but the issue of location is really something that every engineer should design. The second issue of sanitary design is the issue of "light." At first glance, this issue does not seem to have much to do with the lives of ordinary people. In fact, this is not the case. The issue of "light" can shift the entire body and mind's happiness, and it is enough to affect the entire body's nerves and health. We have to engage in meticulous design. Light can be roughly divided into two categories, namely natural sunlight and artificial light. South-facing residences have the best light, so designers should try to open windows facing south as much as possible to introduce a large amount of sunlight, which not only comforts people's body and mind, but also kills mold in the air. The windows in other directions should pay attention to the appropriate area during the design, and the proper color arrangement of the wall decoration will improve your light, which is also something that should be paid attention to. (To be continued) Architectural Jargon (5) Mei Zhenhuan | About the use in the construction site | Grass Oil | (Prime Coat) When the painter applies the first coat of paint on the hall or other utensils, it is called grass oil. Drier | (Prier) If the paint requires its inherent quick-drying properties, then it can only be mixed with some drier. A drier is a very dry substance. Middle Transom | What is a middle transom (Tram son)? It is a horizontal transom that separates the waist (Fan Light) and the door (Door) of the hall. Stile | It is a term for a kind of material in the organization of doors and windows. It is divided into middle stile (Lock Style), side stile (Side style) and other names. Rail | Rail is also a term for a kind of material in the organization of doors and windows. It has top rail (Top Rail), middle rail (Lock Rail), and bottom rail (Bottom Rail). In addition to this, there are many kinds of terms for the materials on doors and windows, such as panel, concave line, and betel nut. Door Stop | (Door Stop) (Fearing that the handle of the door (Handle), whether it is made of porcelain, glass or copper, may sometimes be damaged by a strong push, or may damage the plaster on the wall, so a bump stop is nailed on the floor (Floor) or skirting (Skirting) to prevent the force. It is made of wood and the shape is square or round. Tie Bar | Scaffolding is built on the base of tall buildings. When building, because the length of bamboo or wood is not enough, it must be built layer by layer. The horizontal one is called a tie bar, and the vertical ones are called sky-piercing, the one that puts the scaffolding board is called horizontal rib, and the two intersecting ones that prevent shaking are called throwing support. These all belong to the scaffolding. Scratch Coat | The first coat of plaster applied by the plasterer on the wall is called scratch coat. Ordinary clay mud is mostly used, and yellow sand clay mud is also used, but this is not commonly used for ordinary street houses. Set Back | (Set Back) If the height of the house or the width of the road line exceeds the regulations of the Public Works Bureau's construction code: it must be set back (for example, the road is set back a few feet, the house is set back a few feet), and the large square foot under the wall (Footing) is initially wider than the wall, and then it is gradually reduced, which is also called set back (for example, set back twenty inches, set back fifteen inches.) Floating Bridge | (Moving) The most difficult thing in the construction site is transporting materials. When the first floor of the house is built, it is necessary to rely on the floating bridge to place the joist. (To be continued) Solicitation of Standard Designs for the West Lake Architectural Scenic Area A. Construction Site The four mountains and plains of West Lake, limited to those that can be seen from West Lake. B. Scope of Drawings ㈠ Residential Buildings Whether for rent or for self-occupation, they must be isolated. ㈡ Public Buildings Such as assembly halls, hotels, theaters, etc., must have surrounding courtyards. C. Design Standards ㈠ Style Regardless of Eastern or Western style, as long as it is suitable for the location and environment, and does not go against landscape art. ㈡ Color Take bright colors without being vulgar, and plain colors without being dull, and must be suitable for the environment. ㈢ Height Mountain buildings shall not exceed two floors, and flat ground shall not exceed three floors. The height of each floor shall be limited to 4 to 5 meters, except for palace-style buildings, but all shall be limited to those that do not obstruct scenic spots. ㈣ Cost The cost shall not be too high compared to the current market price, so as to conform to the current social and economic conditions. D. Key Points of the Design ㈠ Each type of drawing must have a floor plan, floor plan, roof plan, front view, and cross-sectional view. It is best if the scenery can be expressed with a bird's-eye view. The dimensions are all in meters. ㈡ Applicants should indicate the building materials and exterior colors, or provide a separate description. ㈢ The exterior decoration and equipment of the house and the location should be drawn in detail. ㈣ The submitted designs must comply with the Hangzhou City building regulations. ㈤ The size of the drawing paper should be 60 cm long and 90 cm wide, and the scale should be 1/50. It should be drawn clearly with a pen and written in Chinese except for the dimensions. E. Solicitation Method ㈠ The Hangzhou Municipal Government shall send letters to domestic architects and publish advertisements to solicit designs. Applicants must submit the drawings and descriptions to the Municipal Government's Engineering Department before March 1st of the 24th year. After the Municipal Government hires experts to convene a public review on a regular basis, applicants shall only write symbols on the drawings, and their names, addresses, and the symbols used shall be sent to the Municipal Government in separate sealed letters, which will be opened after the designs are approved. ㈡ All submitted designs that are selected will not be returned, and the Hangzhou Municipal Government may print and publish the selected designs and descriptions, indicating the names of the selected persons in a special booklet for citizens to refer to when building. ㈢ For each type of selected design, the Municipal Government will award the top three names, and each will receive a bonus of 200 yuan, 100 yuan, and 50 yuan in order.

Shen Bao Local Supplement Film Supplement Bette Davis on the Lessons Hollywood Taught Her Shu Min Bette Davis, the female lead in "Of Human Bondage," was mistaken for a woman who hated women after performing in "Bondage." Because she performed so deeply, people who watched "Bondage" hated the shameless waitress in it and despised women in general. In fact, she was just acting as much as possible, vividly and realistically. She herself is a woman, she also has girlfriends, how could she hate women? Bette is not only a keen observer. She is also one of the most clear-headed women in Hollywood. Her art is not superficial imitation, but personal experience. Her family life is also very rational, which is unique in Hollywood. Her husband, Harmon Nelson, is a pianist in a hotel. She herself is a star, earning about $1,000 a week. But her family living expenses are based on her husband's salary, and she lives within her means. She herself goes to the studio every day in a large new car. That is a must according to her star status. But usually when she goes out to play with her husband, she sits with her husband in a broken car. This is what makes her special, and what ordinary people in Hollywood are unwilling to do. But her reasons are very sufficient, and not entirely on saving, although that is also very important. A female actor's days are very short. She has to try to save money in preparation for the future. But Bette's biggest reason is not just saving money. She said that all self-loving men have a sense of self-respect and independence, and do not like to rely on women's income for a living. She herself is a female star, and her husband is a pianist with a low position, but she does not want him to feel inferior in his profession. She always wants her husband to know that it is not he who relies on her, but she who relies on him. The man is the head of the family and should bear the economic responsibility of the family. Therefore, the common living expenses of their family are borne by her husband, but each of them also has their own private accounts. I'm afraid I've talked too much nonsense. What I want to say here is that Bette has keen observation and rich experience. Because of keen observation and rich experience, there is thorough understanding and rational action. The following are some lessons she said she learned from Hollywood, which can be used as a life lesson for general film practitioners: Living in Hollywood is like living anywhere else, and personal harmony is essential. If you live in a completely ideal, utopian world, then you can enjoy absolute freedom, do whatever you want, and say whatever you want. But our world is not an ideal world. Therefore, we must harmonize with reality and the environment, no matter where you are. But there is one difference in Hollywood: it is very easy for a person to harmonize too much, lose himself, and become part of Hollywood. In short, it is to lose your own personality. This may be because you have trained yourself too harshly in the glory of the film industry. When you get to Hollywood, the first lesson you will learn is to restrain your temper. You must be able to endure being punished, harshly criticized, and all kinds of insults, and remember that they are all beneficial to your career and art. In this peace of mind to endure, you often over-compromise, follow anyone's will, lose your own judgment, and lose your own personality. "Also, the easiest problem to make in Hollywood is the loss of sincerity, because if you live in Hollywood for a long time, you will learn that personal opinions cannot be expressed arbitrarily. In this way, it often flows into hypocrisy. "In Hollywood, you cannot expect the outside world to praise your work. Therefore, to compensate for that lack, you cannot but have your own appreciation. However, unless you understand yourself, you often become arrogant or use affected forms to create special images in others. "You must realize the necessity of thrift early on, and not spend all of your income. The greatest danger in Hollywood is that when you earn a lot of money, you feel extremely embarrassed to spend less money, which is not in line with your status. In fact, it is all caused by the drive of an unconscious vanity. You must understand how long your high salary will last. It is based on the public's preferences, and the public's preferences are extremely unreliable and sometimes incomprehensible. "From the first day you step into the film industry, you must be close to the press, treat the representatives of the press honestly and without deception, and provide them with real news. This does not mean that you must use the people in the press to promote yourself. Their advice and criticism, whether printed on paper or delivered in person, is worthy of your humble acceptance. Film Review "College Life" Ji Han Bachelor Arts - Cathay With a slightly satirical stance, using the thoughts, lives, and dynamics of college students as the theme, and giving vulgar sermons to young students, this is to explain the essence of "College Life." In more detail, the playwright's views are very ordinary. He said that a student from a wealthy family should study hard, not waste money, be able to endure hardship, and do his best to help the poor professor couple, but must not believe in socialism, and may as well fall in love with a working girl. On the other hand, he wrote about a female student who earns her own income to study, and she falls in love with a wealthy son, and makes the wealthy son sincerely love her. In order to emphasize his thematic sermon, he described the followers of socialism in a satirical way as being either bookworms or agitators, and when the wealthy son wore a top hat to attend a gathering of socialist believers, he immediately gave him a punishment. As for the students who specialize in pleasure-seeking, they are naturally also ridiculed. It is gratifying that the American college student group is very vividly sketched, but it teaches the students in the turbulent era to live an ordinary life. The success of this sketch is a kind of evil effect of cuteness. In other words, precisely because it makes people feel cute, it gives the audience a bad influence. Yes, people will feel a little lightness in this film, but the dullness exceeds the lightness. Separating the technical aspects, then from the director to the actors, they all show vulgarity. We do not despise the male and female protagonists because of their lack of fame, but in fact their acting skills are very unfamiliar. Relatively speaking, the male protagonist is more skilled than the female protagonist. The Hair Braid Issue in "Red Sheep Biography" Yi The sound giant film "The Legend of the Red Sheep Hero," which cost more than 100,000 yuan and took ten months to produce, has now been completed and is scheduled to be released. The production of this film is completely different from the dance hero drama. All costumes and backgrounds strive to be true to the situation at that time. The management and layout have taken a lot of thought. However, there is one point that has to be slightly contrary to the facts. Originally, in the former Qing Dynasty, people each had a hair braid, hanging behind their heads, which was extremely ugly in shape. Westerners therefore added the words "pig tail" to ridicule it. Now, the screen characters in "The Legend of the Red Sheep" do not have the special decoration of hair braids, because this hair braid is detrimental to the national image. After comparison, it is felt that the national image is insulted, and the relationship is not shallow. Slightly contrary to the facts is a minor matter. Moreover, the actions of the screen characters are mostly frontal and less reverse, and the cancellation of the hair braid does not cause a strange feeling. It is said that the staff of Xinhua Company had many discussions on the hair braid issue before they resolutely cancelled it. "Empty Valley Orchid" Song Giveaway The

Boy Scout Ni Bingyao of This City Walks Across All of Zhejiang and Returns to Shanghai 204

Lasting Over a Month, Passing Through More Than Ten Counties

Mr. Ni Bingyao, a member of the Wu Yu Boy Scout Corps of the Sixth, Seventh, and Eighth Regiments of the Chinese Boy Scouts, determined to walk across all of Zhejiang. He trekked thousands of miles and set off at the end of last year, passing through Hang County, Yuyao, Fenghua, Yin County, Huangyan, Zhoushan, Taizhou, and other places. He conducted on-the-spot research and investigation into the local rural economy and the state of Boy Scout education. He will record his impressions in detail in a manual. Once it has been refined and polished, he plans to contribute it to the Boy Scout community of the entire city as a reference. Mr. Ni returned to Shanghai on the 27th of this month. He told a Shanghai News Agency reporter yesterday that he received generous treatment from the local military, political, and academic circles in the places he passed through, and also received inscriptions and signatures from celebrities as souvenirs. As for the goals of this trip: (1) To broaden his knowledge and understanding of the rural conditions in the Chinese interior; (2) To encourage the interest in activities of those who come later, hoping that there will be frequent excursions in the Boy Scout world in the future. It is said that all members of the Wu Yu Corps held a banquet for Mr. Ni last night at the Southeast Hongyun Restaurant to welcome him back, and the corps leader presented him with a medal on the spot.

Boy Scout First Shooting Practice at Municipal Chamber of Commerce Achieves Excellent Results 205

Since the Boy Scout Corps of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce began military training, it has been extremely serious about both academic and training subjects. The other day, it specially dispatched the first group of fifteen trainees to Pudong for live ammunition shooting practice. Each member shot six bullets, and as many as eleven of them hit the target completely. Among them, Hu Chengji of the Standing Army Corps ranked first, Qi Shizhang ranked second, and Zhang Lie ranked third, etc., in terms of results.

The Circumstances of Principal Jia of Zhaohe Resigning 206

The sudden resignation of Jia Botao, the principal of Zhaohe Middle School, was reported in yesterday's newspaper. The reporter specially visited him yesterday. According to Mr. Jia, the establishment of Zhaohe Middle School was jointly initiated by Mayor Wu, Director Yang, and advanced figures from the Party-State and society. He had put in a lot of effort. However, because he felt that he was not particularly good at education, even though he was cautious in his daily work and worked hard to develop the school, he was deeply afraid of increasing his guilt. Therefore, he had long wanted to get out of it. However, it was not easy to convene the board of directors, and the various funds were not yet settled, so he could not bear to leave. Now, fortunately, the central government's subsidies have been successively issued, the various equipment and scale are roughly prepared, and land acquisition and construction have also been carried out. After several years of running around, fortunately, there has been no mishap. Therefore, taking advantage of the change of semesters, he resolutely resigned, and handed over all school equipment, documents, seals, books, instruments, and deposits to Vice Chairman Yang for inventory. He firmly believed that future leaders would be able to maintain the glorious history of the past and work harder. He hoped that the old colleagues and students would work and study with peace of mind and jointly open up a bright future. This would be the school's fortune and also his great comfort.

Progress of Minli Girls' Middle School 207

Since the new four-story steel-framed concrete school building of Nan Shi Minli Girls' Middle School was completed last year, all equipment has been even more perfect than before. Now, it is even more determined to make progress according to the planned plan. In terms of education, applied subjects are increased and the latest teaching methods are adopted. In terms of moral education, the New Life Movement is vigorously implemented, and special attention is paid to cultivating habits of discipline, politeness, hard work, endurance, sincerity, frugality, and simplicity. The spring enrollment is scheduled to be held on the morning of the 31st of this month. It is said that the number of applicants has already exceeded the planned quota.
